and \u0026#34;Virtual Reality,\u0026#34; as part of their control and narrative-shaping strategy.","author":"Ananya Gairola","created_at":"2023-06-16T10:10:32Z","updated_at":"2023-06-16T10:10:32Z","url":"https://www.benzinga.com/23/06/32889236/the-words-apple-never-utters-during-an-event-mkbhd-breaks-it-down","content":"\u003cp\u003eTech YouTuber \u003cstrong\u003eMarques Brownlee\u003c/strong\u003e AKA \u003cstrong\u003eMKBHD\u003c/strong\u003e, has shed some light on \u003cstrong\u003eApple Inc.'s\u003c/strong\u003e (NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/AAPL#NASDAQ\"\u003eAAPL\u003c/a\u003e) unique approach to presentations, highlighting the words that the tech giant deliberately avoids using — especially when on stage\u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/news/large-cap/23/06/32723259/watchos-10-unveiled-at-wwdc-2023-apple-reinvents-the-smartwatch-experience\"\u003e, like during the WWDC event\u003c/a\u003e. \u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhat Happened:\u003c/strong\u003e\u0026nbsp;In a YouTube video, MKBHD analyzed Apple\u0026#8217;s presentations over the years and discovered a pattern of words that the company consistently avoids or rarely mentions.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eIn the video, Brownlee said that \u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/news/large-cap/23/06/32721949/apple-unveils-ios-17-and-ipados-17-at-wwdc-2023-introduces-new-standby-mode-and-more\"\u003eduring Apple\u0026#8217;s latest event\u003c/a\u003e, the Worldwide Developers Conference, which showcased their new Vision Pro headset, the company representatives not once utter the phrase \u0026#8220;virtual reality\u0026#8221; on stage, despite it being a core feature of the product.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eSee Also:\u0026nbsp;\u003c/em\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/news/23/06/32869484/whats-apples-next-big-iphone-camera-trick-vision-pro-may-offer-a-clue\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"\u003e\u003cem\u003eWhat\u0026#8217;s Apple\u0026#8217;s Next Big iPhone Camera Trick? Vision Pro May Offer A Clue\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eHere are some words that, according to Brownlee, Apple deliberately refrains from speaking on a public forum: \u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAI or Artificial Intelligence: \u003c/strong\u003eOne notable word absent from Apple\u0026#8217;s presentations is \u0026#8220;Artificial Intelligence\u0026#8221; or \"AI.\" \u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/news/large-cap/23/05/32324579/google-io-2023-highlights-ai-progress-palm-2-challenges-chatgpt-and-introduces-cutting-edge-ai-pow\"\u003eWhile other companies\u003c/a\u003e, like \u003cstrong\u003eAlphabet Inc. \u003c/strong\u003e(NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/GOOG#NASDAQ\"\u003eGOOG\u003c/a\u003e) (NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/GOOGL#NASDAQ\"\u003eGOOGL\u003c/a\u003e), openly embrace and discuss AI, Apple prefers to use phrases like \u0026#8220;machine learning\u0026#8221; and \u0026#8220;ML\u0026#8221; to describe their technologies.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eVirtual Reality or VR: \u003c/strong\u003eApple\u0026#8217;s strategic avoidance of the term \u0026#8220;virtual reality\u0026#8221; for their Vision Pro headset is part of a greater narrative-shaping effort. Instead of \u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/news/23/06/32730028/how-does-apples-vision-pro-compare-with-metas-quest-3\"\u003elabeling it as a VR headset\u003c/a\u003e, Apple positions the device as an augmented reality experience. \u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eBy using terms like \u0026#8220;environments\u0026#8221; and refraining from explicitly mentioning VR, Apple intends to guide consumer perception, said MKBHD. They aim to differentiate the headset and steer the narrative towards AR, aligning with their broader ambitions in the AR space.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eOther Words: \u003c/strong\u003eDuring presentations, Apple is known for not explicitly mentioning certain technical details. Instead, Apple focuses on subjective attributes and introduces branded terms to describe their features. For example, they refer to a \u0026#8220;Taptic Engine\u0026#8221; instead of a large linear vibration motor and use the word \u0026#8220;ceramic shield\u0026#8221; to describe their supplier\u0026#8217;s latest version of glass. \u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhy It's Important:\u0026nbsp;\u003c/strong\u003eAccording to the YouTuber, Apple\u0026#8217;s omission of certain words is rooted in their desire for control and avoidance of comparison. By refraining from associating new products with commonly used terms, the company mitigates the risk of \u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/opinion/23/06/32843214/i-made-them-up-googles-ai-tool-admits-to-falsifying-information-apologizes-to-reporter\"\u003enegative sentiments impacting its reputation\u003c/a\u003e.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eWatch the complete video here:\u0026nbsp;\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cfigure class=\"wp-block-embed is-type-video is-provider-youtube wp-block-embed-youtube wp-embed-aspect-16-9 wp-has-aspect-ratio\"\u003e\u003cdiv class=\"wp-block-embed__wrapper\"\u003e\n\u003ciframe loading=\"lazy\" title=\"Apple\u0026#039;s Forbidden Words\" width=\"500\" height=\"281\" src=\"https://www.youtube.com/embed/kvN5_GXlg2Y?feature=oembed\" frameborder=\"0\" allow=\"accelerometer; autoplay; clipboard-write; encrypted-media; gyroscope; picture-in-picture; web-share\" allowfullscreen\u003e\u003c/iframe\u003e\n\u003c/div\u003e\u003c/figure\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eCheck out more of Benzinga\u0026#8217;s Consumer Tech coverage by\u0026nbsp;\u003c/em\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/topic/consumer-tech\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"\u003e\u003cem\u003efollowing this link\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cem\u003e.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eRead Next:\u0026nbsp;\u003c/em\u003e\u003ca target=\"_blank\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/news/23/06/32840505/apples-flagship-headphones-are-now-99-off-on-amazon-at-450\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\"\u003e\u003cem\u003eApple\u0026#8217;s Flagship Headphones Are Now $99 Off On Amazon At $450\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","symbols":["AAPL","GOOG","GOOGL"],"source":"benzinga"}]

(NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/AAPL#NASDAQ\"\u003eAAPL\u003c/a\u003e)\u003c/strong\u003e has won a patent that should make future iPhones scratch resistant.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhat Happened:\u003c/strong\u003e Apple has won a patent intended to make future iPhones so scratch resistant you would not have to put them in a case, \u003ca href=\"https://www.patentlyapple.com/2023/06/apple-wins-a-patent-for-an-abrasion-resistant-back-panel-made-of-glass-or-metal-for-possible-future-iphones-ipads-macbooks-1.html\"\u003ereported\u003c/a\u003e Patently Apple.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eSee Also: \u003c/em\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/news/23/06/32874907/a-declined-autograph-letter-with-steve-jobs-signature-fetches-its-owner-480-000\"\u003e\u003cem\u003eA Declined Autograph Letter With Steve Jobs\u0026#8217; Signature Fetches Its Owner $480,000\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eMost modern smartphones have a chassis made of metal or glass. These materials are prone to issues of their own – while metal chassis is prone to dents, glass back often cracks when users with clumsy hands eventually drop them. Plastic material is prone to both scratches and dents.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eThat leaves companies with one option – using a mix that combines the strengths of multiple materials. Apple's solution is a combination of metal and ceramic.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\"The abrasion-resistant members may be formed from metal or ceramic. The substrate comprises a moldable matrix. The abrasion-resistant members are harder than the moldable matrix,\" Apple said in its patent filing.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eTo illustrate how it might look in practice, Apple's patent includes a diagram that shows a series of \"beads\" in a rectangular pattern. These beads are spaced at 10 to 100 microns from each other, but the distance should largely be imperceptible.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eWill this be the cure for clumsy hands destroying iPhones? Time will tell, but it looks like Apple certainly is trying to find a fix.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eCheck out more of Benzinga\u0026#8217;s Consumer Tech coverage by \u003c/em\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/topic/consumer-tech\"\u003e\u003cem\u003efollowing this link\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003cem\u003e.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eRead Next: \u003c/em\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/news/23/06/32891176/snag-the-google-pixel-watch-at-a-big-discount-of-80\"\u003e\u003cem\u003eSnag The Google Pixel Watch At A Big Discount Of $80\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","symbols":["AAPL"],"source":"benzinga"}]

[{"T":"n","id":32896084,"headline":"Meta\u0026#39;s AI Voicebox Aims To Do For Audio What ChatGPT, Dall-E Did For Text, Image Generation","summary":" ","author":"AJ Fabino","created_at":"2023-06-16T15:59:25Z","updated_at":"2023-06-16T15:59:26Z","url":"https://www.benzinga.com/markets/equities/23/06/32896084/metas-ai-voicebox-aims-to-do-for-audio-what-chatgpt-dall-e-did-for-text-image-generation","content":"\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMeta Platforms Inc\u003c/strong\u003e (NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/META#NASDAQ\"\u003eMETA\u003c/a\u003e) CEO \u003cstrong\u003eMark Zuckerberg\u003c/strong\u003e on Friday introduced Voicebox, a text-to-speech (TTS) \u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/topic/artificial-intelligence\"\u003egenerative artificial intelligence speech model\u003c/a\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhat Happened:\u003c/strong\u003e Voicebox is an advanced AI model that can produce realistic, contextually accurate speech output from given text and has the potential to complete tasks for which it was not explicitly trained. \u003ca href=\"https://www.yahoo.com/news/metas-voicebox-ai-is-a-dall-e-for-text-to-speech-150021287.html\"\u003eEngadget compared\u003c/a\u003e Voicebox to what OpenAI's ChatGPT did for text output and what Dall-E did for image generation.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eZuckerberg made the announcement via his Meta Channel on Instagram, accompanied by a video showing how Voicebox can convert text into speech in various styles, how it can handle background noise much like an audio eraser and how it can even replace spoken words.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eBuilt on a foundation of \u0026#8220;non-autoregressive flow-matching model trained to infill speech, given audio context and text,\" Engadget noted Voicebox\u0026#8217;s training involved more than 50,000 hours of diverse, unfiltered audio in multiple languages, including English, French, Spanish, German, Polish and Portuguese.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eVoicebox leverages its varied training to deliver conversationally fluid speech in various languages. In tests, speech recognition models trained on synthetic speech generated by Voicebox performed nearly as well as models trained on real speech, the report said, showing a 1% degradation in error rate.\u003cbr\u003e\u003cbr\u003e\u003cem\u003eRead also: \u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/news/23/06/32889872/meta-opens-new-ai-software-for-commercial-use-a-bold-move-set-to-rival-google-and-microsoft\"\u003eMeta Opens New AI Software For Commercial Use, A Bold Move Set to Rival Google and Microsoft\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhy It Matters:\u003c/strong\u003e One of Voicebox\u0026#8217;s defining characteristics is its ability to edit audio clips actively, as it can eliminate noise from speech and replace misspoken words. By identifying a noisy segment in the speech, the user can crop it and instruct the model to regenerate the segment, much like using image-editing software to enhance photos.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eUnlike existing TTS generators, Voicebox doesn\u0026#8217;t require extensive source material to mimic a subject. It\u0026#8217;s the result of Meta\u0026#8217;s zero-shot text-to-speech training method known as Flow Matching.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eWhile the potential applications of Voicebox are nearly endless, Meta decided not to release the app or its source code to the public as of now due to potential misuse concerns according to Engadget. \u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eMETA Price Action:\u003c/strong\u003e Shares of Meta are trading 0.92% higher to $284.42 at last check, according to Benzinga Pro.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eRead next: \u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/general/entertainment/23/06/32892926/benzingas-stock-whisper-index-5-stocks-investors-are-secretly-monitoring-but-not-talking-ab\"\u003eBenzinga\u0026#8217;s \u0026#8216;Stock Whisper\u0026#8217; Index: 5 Stocks Investors Are Secretly Monitoring But Not Talking About Yet\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003ePhoto via Pixabay. \u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e","symbols":["META"],"source":"benzinga"}]

Android malware \u003cstrong\u003eGravityRAT\u003c/strong\u003e is back and is now targeting the \u003cstrong\u003eMeta Platforms Inc.-owned (NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/META#NASDAQ\"\u003eMETA\u003c/a\u003e)\u003c/strong\u003e WhatsApp's backup files from unsuspecting users' phones.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhat Happened:\u003c/strong\u003e An updated version of notorious Android malware GravityRAT is now out in the open, targeting unsuspecting users and stealing the WhatsApp backup files stored on their phones.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eSee Also: \u003c/em\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/news/23/06/32912056/how-to-generate-instagram-post-backgrounds-using-midjourney\"\u003e\u003cem\u003eHow To Generate Instagram Post Backgrounds Using Midjourney\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eGravityRAT is a trojan that first surfaced in 2015. According to Facebook researchers, a Pakistan-based group named SpaceCobra is suspected to be behind this malware. Since August 2022, it has been distributed via two other messaging applications: \u003cstrong\u003eBingeChat and Chatico\u003c/strong\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eWhy Is It Important:\u003c/strong\u003e GravityRAT is a remote access trojan. As the name suggests, it provides remote access to hackers, allowing them to access and exfiltrate sensitive information like call logs, contacts, messages, locations, photos, videos, and even documents.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eIn this instance, GravityRAT extracts WhatsApp backup files and if they are not end-to-end encrypted, they can be easily extracted to get complete access to all the messages, photos, videos, documents, and other media items stored in the backup file.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eHow To Stay Safe:\u003c/strong\u003e When it comes to staying safe from malware on Android, the best solution is not to sideload applications, especially those from non-reputable sources.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eWhile \u003cstrong\u003eAlphabet Inc.'s (NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/GOOGL#NASDAQ\"\u003eGOOGL\u003c/a\u003e) Google\u003c/strong\u003e has the \u003cstrong\u003ePlay Protect\u003c/strong\u003e safety feature built into Android, it is not a full-proof solution, and users should download apps from the \u003cstrong\u003ePlay Store\u003c/strong\u003e to remain safe.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\n\n\u003cp\u003eAdditionally, WhatsApp also has the option to enable \u003cstrong\u003eend-to-end encryption\u003c/strong\u003e on backups. [{"T":"n","id":32924098,"headline":"AMD Promises An AI Chip Power Shift","summary":"Last Tuesday, Advanced Micro Devices Inc (NASDAQ: AMD) unveiled a new chip that holds the promise to be the biggest threat to date to the monopoly of the AI chip market leader, Nvidia Corporation (NASDAQ: NVDA).","author":"Upwallstreet","created_at":"2023-06-20T13:43:20Z","updated_at":"2023-06-20T13:43:20Z","url":"https://www.benzinga.com/23/06/32924098/amd-promises-an-ai-chip-power-shift","content":"\u003cp\u003eLast Tuesday, Advanced Micro Devices Inc (NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/AMD#NASDAQ\"\u003eAMD\u003c/a\u003e) unveiled a new chip that holds the promise to be the biggest threat to date to the monopoly of the AI chip market leader, Nvidia Corporation (NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/NVDA#NASDAQ\"\u003eNVDA\u003c/a\u003e). GPUs are undoubtedly powering the AI race, as these chips are used by OpenAI that built ChatGPT which seems to have started all the hype and certainly brought in a lot of good vibes to Microsoft Corporation (NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/MSFT#NASDAQ\"\u003eMSFT\u003c/a\u003e).\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003ch3\u003eThe\u0026nbsp;MI300X\u003c/h3\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eTargeted as a competitor to H100 GPU from Nvidia,\u0026nbsp;AMD\u0026rsquo;s forthcoming most-advanced GPU for artificial intelligence applications is expected to arrive to customers later this year. Its CDNA architecture is designed for large language models that use lots of memory as well as other cutting-edge AI models. AMD did not disclose any pricing details but lower pricing will not only put a price pressure on Nvidia whose\u0026nbsp;H100 comes at\u0026nbsp;$30,000 or more, but also have a deep impact on the development of generative AI applications that are high in cost.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003ch3\u003eThe AI Opportunity And Untapped Market\u003c/h3\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eWhile the PC market struggles to get out of its post-pandemic slump,\u0026nbsp;CEO Lisa Su\u0026nbsp;finds AI to be AMD\u0026rsquo;s largest and by far the biggest strategic long-term growth opportunity.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eAccording to Analysts, AMD is certainly one of the greatest challenges to Nvidia especially with this new release that AMD will sell to everybody, but the key of its success remains lies in how many developers will want to use it. For example, AI developers preferred Nvidia chips due to a well-developed software package CUDA that enabled them to access the chip\u0026rsquo;s core hardware features. But AMD\u0026nbsp;revealed on Tuesday it made its own software for its AI chips, ROCm.\u0026nbsp;If developers embrace AMD\u0026rsquo;s chips, named by the company as accelerators, as a substitute for those made by Nvidia, the AI chip market is certainly in for a power shift and AMD is in for a turnaround as its current brand identity is tied to traditional computer processors. Reuters reported that Amazon.com Inc (NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/AMZN#NASDAQ\"\u003eAMZN\u003c/a\u003e) is considering AMD\u0026rsquo;s chips but still hasn\u0026rsquo;t decided which chips will power its AI efforts, however Amazon has not made any public commitments.\u0026nbsp;Dave Brown, vice president of elastic compute cloud at Amazon,\u0026nbsp;did state that AMD and AWS teams are working together, while Amazon declined to work with Nvidia on the\u0026nbsp;DGX Cloud offering. But, it is common knowledge that Amazon, more precisely AWS, likes to design its serves from the ground up. For example, when it started selling H100 chips that Nvidia makes, it did it as part of its design.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003ch3\u003eIntel Is The Living Proof That Future Is Promised To No One\u003c/h3\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eOn Friday, Intel Corporation (NASDAQ:\u003ca class=\"ticker\" href=\"https://www.benzinga.com/stock/INTC#NASDAQ\"\u003eINTC\u003c/a\u003e) revealed\u0026nbsp;it will be commiting\u0026nbsp;$4.6 billion in its new chip assembly and test facility in Poland as part of its plan to build capacity across three continents and restore its chip making leadership position. Last year, Intel announced it will be building a massive chip complex in Germany, as well as facilities in Ireland and France. Intel also announced yesterday that after 15 years, it is rebranding its consumer CPU. With a simplified naming scheme that focuses on its Core branding, many have noticed the new looks somewhat similar to AMD\u0026rsquo;s Ryzen naming scheme. After being the unquestioned leader with an almost market monopoly for over a decade, Intel is no longer fighting only against AMD who was its chief rival but also with Nvidia who took absolute charge because it was the first to enter the AI game and it did it early. But as Google and Amazon design their own chips, even Nvidia will be facing increased competition.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003ch3\u003eAMD\u0026#39;s AI Journey Could Be A\u0026nbsp;Game-changing One\u003c/h3\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003eAMD president Victor Pen\u0026nbsp;admitted that this is a journey but assured AMD has made great progress in building a powerful product that works with various systems, models, libraries and frameworks. All in all, it seems like AMD\u0026rsquo;s newest chips have the potential to\u0026nbsp;redefine the AI chip landscape.\u0026nbsp;\u003c/p\u003e\r\n\r\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cem\u003eDISCLAIMER: This content is for informational purposes only. It is not intended as investing advice.\u003c/em\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\r\n ","symbols":["AMD","AMZN","INTC","MSFT","NVDA"],"source":"benzinga"}]

[{"T":"n","id":32926909,"headline":"\u0026#39;Bernie Sanders Launches Senate Investigation Into Amazon Labor Practices\u0026#39; - Washington Post","summary":"https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/2023/06/20/sanders-investigation-sentate-amazon/\n\nSen. Bernie Sanders (I-Vt.), chair of the influential Senate committee on health, education, labor and pension, launched an","author":"Happy Mohamed","created_at":"2023-06-20T14:46:49Z","updated_at":"2023-06-20T14:46:49Z","url":"https://www.benzinga.com/news/23/06/32926909/bernie-sanders-launches-senate-investigation-into-amazon-labor-practices-washington-post","content":"\u003cp\u003e\u003ca href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/2023/06/20/sanders-investigation-sentate-amazon/\" title=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/2023/06/20/sanders-investigation-sentate-amazon/\"\u003ehttps://www.washingtonpost.com/business/2023/06/20/sanders-investigation-sentate-amazon/\u003c/a\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSen. Bernie Sanders (I-Vt.), chair of the influential Senate committee on health, education, labor and pension, launched an investigation this week into the nation\u0026rsquo;s second-largest employer, Amazon, and the working conditions inside its warehouses.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eIn a letter to Amazon chief executive Andy Jassy, the Vermont senator demanded information about the company\u0026rsquo;s \u0026ldquo;systematically underreported\u0026rdquo; injury rates, turnover, productivity targets and adherence to federal and state safety recommendations. Sanders has often castigated Amazon in fervent speeches on income inequality and corporate greed in America.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026ldquo;Amazon sets an example for the rest of the country,\u0026rdquo; Sanders told The Washington Post in an interview about his decision to focus on the e-commerce giant. \u0026ldquo;What Amazon does, their attitude, their lack of respect for workers permeates the American corporate world.\u0026rdquo;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eAmazon founder Jeff Bezos owns The Post. Interim Post chief executive Patty Stonesifer sits on Amazon\u0026rsquo;s board.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSanders\u0026rsquo;s Amazon probe is the latest in a series of investigations that the self-proclaimed socialist and two-time presidential candidate has launched since assuming his role as chairman of the Senate HELP Committee in January. The position has given him vast authority to direct national attention to the practices of some of the country\u0026rsquo;s most powerful companies, such as Starbucks and Moderna, and to interrogate their corporate leaders.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eAn investigation into workplace health and safety practices at Amazon \u0026mdash; the e-commerce giant that has drawn attention for opposing union organizing efforts and for injury rates\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://www.google.com/search?q=injury+rates+amazon+washington+post\u0026amp;sxsrf=APwXEdfTXEL3LUp_NeMyX2LtOtuBSJwo-g%3A1686952466151\u0026amp;ei=EtqMZKnjCLmpptQPltussAo\u0026amp;ved=0ahUKEwiptP3T48j_AhW5lIkEHZYtC6YQ4dUDCBA\u0026amp;uact=5\u0026amp;oq=injury+rates+amazon+washington+post\u0026amp;gs_lcp=Cgxnd3Mtd2l6LXNlcnAQAzIFCCEQoAEyBQghEKsCMgUIIRCrAjoECAAQRzoGCAAQFhAeOggIABCKBRCGA0oECEEYAFBkWP8MYI0OaABwAngAgAGcAYgBxAqSAQQxNS4xmAEAoAEBwAEByAEI\u0026amp;sclient=gws-wiz-serp\u0026amp;bshm=nce/1\" target=\"_blank\"\u003eroughly double\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;the industry average \u0026mdash; gives Sanders an outlet to push for accountability from one of the country\u0026rsquo;s most influential employers amid a party split Congress.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSteve Kelly, a spokesperson for Amazon responded that the company had \u0026ldquo;received Chairman Sanders\u0026rsquo; letter this evening and are in the early stages of reviewing it.\u0026rdquo; He noted that Amazon had an open invitation for Sanders to tour one of Amazon\u0026rsquo;s warehouses.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eThe HELP committee\u0026rsquo;s previous major target was Starbucks. In January, Sanders wrote a similar letter to Starbucks founder and former CEO Howard Schultz, accusing the company of refusing to bargain a contract with workers who voted to unionize. In March, Schulz testified before the congressional committee under threat of subpoena from Sanders. \u0026ldquo;Over the past 18 months, Starbucks has waged the most aggressive and illegal union-busting campaign in the modern history of our country,\u0026rdquo; Sanders said at the hearing.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eA Starbucks spokesperson\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/2023/03/24/starbucks-union-shareholder-howard-schultz-bargaining/?itid=lk_inline_manual_16\" target=\"_blank\"\u003esaid at the time\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;that Starbucks had not attempted to delay bargaining and that the company has come to the table as legally obligated at stores that have voted to unionize.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eRegarding whether the senator intends to call Amazon\u0026rsquo;s Jassy or founder Bezos to testify in a similar hearing, Sanders said, \u0026ldquo;that\u0026rsquo;s an absolute possibility.\u0026rdquo;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eIn his letter to Jassy, Sanders describes Amazon\u0026rsquo;s warehouse conditions as \u0026ldquo;uniquely dangerous.\u0026rdquo; He pointed to a recent report compiled by a coalition of labor unions using federal data that found Amazon\u0026rsquo;s serious injury rate was double the warehouse industry average in 2021. He also cited government investigations that found health and safety violations at Amazon facilities, and his own conversations with Amazon warehouse workers.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026ldquo;Amazon is one of the most valuable companies in the world, worth $1.3 trillion and its founder, Jeff Bezos, is one of the richest men in the world worth nearly $150 billion,\u0026rdquo; Sanders wrote. \u0026ldquo;Amazon should be one of the safest places in America to work, not one of the most dangerous.\u0026rdquo;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eKelly, the company spokesperson, said that Amazon has recorded a 23 percent reduction in injuries since 2019, and pointed to a past statement about Amazon\u0026rsquo;s critics splicing the data \u0026quot;to suit their narrative.\u0026rdquo;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026ldquo;We\u0026rsquo;ve invested more than $1 billion into safety initiatives, projects and programs in the last four years, and we\u0026rsquo;ll continue investing and inventing in this area because nothing is more important than our employees\u0026rsquo; safety,\u0026rdquo; Kelly said.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSanders has long slammed working conditions and pay at Amazon. After a campaign led by Sanders, Amazon in 2018 made a\u0026nbsp;\u003ca href=\"https://www.washingtonpost.com/business/2018/10/02/amazon-announces-it-will-boost-minimum-wage-all-workers-after-facing-criticism/?itid=lk_inline_manual_27\" target=\"_blank\"\u003esurprising announcement:\u003c/a\u003e\u0026nbsp;It would raise its base hourly pay rate to $15, more than twice the national minimum wage.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026ldquo;We listened to our critics, thought hard about what we wanted to do and decided we want to lead,\u0026rdquo; Bezos, who was CEO of Amazon at the time, said in a statement. \u0026ldquo;We\u0026rsquo;re excited about this change and encourage our competitors and other large employers to join us.\u0026rdquo;\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSanders said he was \u0026ldquo;appreciative\u0026rdquo; of Amazon\u0026rsquo;s decision to raise its starting wage in his interview with The Post. But said he has been \u0026ldquo;extremely upset by their vehement anti-union behavior\u0026rdquo; and workplace safety record.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003e\u0026ldquo;The proof is in the pudding,\u0026rdquo; Sanders said, noting the Amazon\u0026rsquo;s high level of attrition. A 2021 New York Times investigation found that the company\u0026rsquo;s turnover rate was roughly 150 percent a year.\u003c/p\u003e\n\n\u003cp\u003eSanders has requested that Jassy and Amazon respond by July 5.\u003c/p\u003e","symbols":["AMZN","SPY"],"source":"benzinga"}]
